# Awesome Elixir [![CI Badge](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir) ⭐ 13,091 | 🐛 10 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-10-12 [![Awesome](https://cdn.rawgit.com/sindresorhus/awesome/d7305f38d29fed78fa85652e3a63e154dd8e8829/media/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome) ⭐ 444,818 | 🐛 76 | 📅 2026-03-09 with stars

A curated list of amazingly awesome Elixir libraries, resources, and shiny things inspired by [awesome-php](https://github.com/ziadoz/awesome-php) ⭐ 32,417 | 🐛 69 | 📅 2026-02-25.

If you think a package should be added, please add a :+1: (`:+1:`) at the according issue or create a new one.

There are [other sites with curated lists of elixir packages](#other-awesome-lists) which you can have a look at.

## Actors

*Libraries and tools for working with actors and such.*

* [spawn](https://github.com/eigr/spawn) ⭐ 367 | 🐛 31 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-10 - Elixir poliglot actors service mesh.
* [pooler](https://github.com/seth/pooler) ⭐ 314 | 🐛 10 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2025-10-06 - An OTP Process Pool Application.
* [bpe](https://github.com/spawnproc/bpe) ⭐ 277 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2026-03-01 - Business Process Engine in Erlang. ([Doc](https://bpe.n2o.dev)).
* [alf](https://github.com/antonmi/ALF) ⭐ 212 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-05-25 - Flow-based Application Layer Framework.
* [poolex](https://github.com/general-CbIC/poolex) ⭐ 85 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-11 - Pure elixir pool manager.

## Algorithms and Data structures

*Libraries and implementations of algorithms and data structures.*

* [flow](https://github.com/dashbitco/flow) ⭐ 1,609 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-02-25 - Computational parallel flows on top of GenStage.
* [witchcraft](https://github.com/expede/witchcraft) ⭐ 1,230 | 🐛 24 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2023-08-28 - Common algebraic structures and functions for Elixir.
* [machinery](https://github.com/joaomdmoura/machinery) ⭐ 566 | 🐛 12 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-05-03 - A state machine library for structs in general, it integrates with Phoenix out of the box.
* [fuse](https://github.com/jlouis/fuse) ⭐ 512 | 🐛 8 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2022-02-15 - This application implements a so-called circuit-breaker for Erlang.
* [matrex](https://github.com/versilov/matrex) ⭐ 489 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-08-03 - A blazing fast matrix library for Elixir/Erlang with C implementation using CBLAS.
* [fsm](https://github.com/sasa1977/fsm) ⭐ 361 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-02-04 - Finite state machine as a functional data structure.
* [monadex](https://github.com/rob-brown/MonadEx) ⭐ 307 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2021-10-27 - Upgrade your Elixir pipelines with monads.
* [exconstructor](https://github.com/appcues/exconstructor) ⭐ 292 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-01-23 - An Elixir library for generating struct constructors that handle external data with ease.
* [loom](https://github.com/asonge/loom) ⭐ 228 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-05-30 - A CRDT library with δ-CRDT support.
* [aja](https://github.com/sabiwara/aja) ⭐ 225 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-10-19 - High performance persistent vectors and ordered maps.
* [datastructures](https://github.com/meh/elixir-datastructures) ⭐ 218 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-03-27 - A collection of protocols, implementations and wrappers to work with data structures.
* [erlang-algorithms](https://github.com/aggelgian/erlang-algorithms) ⭐ 160 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2020-05-01 - Implementations of popular data structures and algorithms.
* [remodel](https://github.com/stavro/remodel) ⭐ 141 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2019-04-03 - An Elixir presenter package used to transform map structures.
* [trie](https://github.com/okeuday/trie) ⭐ 132 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2025-05-18 - Erlang Trie Implementation.
* [emel](https://github.com/mrdimosthenis/emel) ⭐ 115 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Gleam | 📅 2024-09-26 - A simple and functional machine learning library written in elixir.
* [bloomex](https://github.com/gmcabrita/bloomex) ⚠️ Archived - A pure Elixir implementation of Scalable Bloom Filters.
* [parallel\_stream](https://github.com/beatrichartz/parallel_stream) ⭐ 103 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2022-09-17 - A parallel stream implementation for Elixir.
* [ecto\_state\_machine](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_state_machine) ⭐ 100 | 🐛 15 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-03-03 - Finite state machine pattern implemented on Elixir and  adopted for Ecto.
* [merkle\_tree](https://github.com/yosriady/merkle_tree) ⭐ 98 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-01-30 - A Merkle hash tree implementation in Elixir.
* [graphmath](https://github.com/crertel/graphmath) ⭐ 88 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-12-08 - An Elixir library for performing 2D and 3D mathematics.
* [the\_fuzz](https://github.com/smashedtoatoms/the_fuzz) ⭐ 81 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-07-24 - Fuzzy string-matching algorithm implementations.
* [sfmt](https://github.com/jj1bdx/sfmt-erlang/) ⚠️ Archived - SIMD-oriented Fast Mersenne Twister (SFMT) for Erlang.
* [lz4](https://github.com/szktty/erlang-lz4) ⭐ 65 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 C | 📅 2021-12-17 - LZ4 bindings for Erlang for fast data compressing.
* [ecto\_materialized\_path](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_materialized_path) ⭐ 64 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2021-10-08 - Tree structure, hierarchy and ancestry for the ecto models.
* [parex](https://github.com/StevenJL/parex) ⭐ 64 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-07-02 - Parallel Execute (Parex) is an Elixir module for executing multiple (slow) processes in parallel.
* [dataframe](https://github.com/JordiPolo/dataframe) ⭐ 63 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2019-01-12 - Package providing functionality similar to Python's Pandas or R's data.frame().
* [sleeplocks](https://github.com/whitfin/sleeplocks) ⭐ 61 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2025-12-29 - BEAM friendly spinlocks for Elixir/Erlang.
* [exmatrix](https://github.com/a115/exmatrix) ⭐ 58 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2023-04-09 - ExMatrix is a small library for working with matrices, originally developed for testing matrix multiplication in parallel.
* [blocking\_queue](https://github.com/joekain/BlockingQueue) ⭐ 55 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2023-07-07 - BlockingQueue is a simple queue implemented as a GenServer. It has a fixed maximum length established when it is created.
* [conrex](https://github.com/NAISorg/conrex) ⭐ 55 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2022-01-12 - An Elixir implementation of the CONREC algorithm for topographic or isochrone maps.
* [cuid](https://github.com/duailibe/cuid) ⭐ 55 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-07-03 - Collision-resistant ids optimized for horizontal scaling and sequential lookup performance, written in Elixir.
* [cuckoo](https://github.com/gmcabrita/cuckoo) ⚠️ Archived - A pure Elixir implementation of [Cuckoo Filters](https://www.cs.cmu.edu/%7Edga/papers/cuckoo-conext2014.pdf).
* [ratio](https://github.com/Qqwy/elixir-rational) ⭐ 42 | 🐛 7 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-03-15 - Adds Rational Numbers and allows them to be used in common arithmetic operations. Also supports conversion between Floats and Rational Numbers.
* [aruspex](https://github.com/dkendal/aruspex) ⭐ 41 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-07-10 - Aruspex is a configurable constraint solver, written purely in Elixir.
* [gen\_fsm](https://github.com/pavlos/gen_fsm) ⭐ 40 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-03-03 - A generic finite state-machine - Elixir wrapper around OTP's gen\_fsm.
* [murmur](https://github.com/gmcabrita/murmur) ⚠️ Archived - A pure Elixir implementation of the non-cryptographic hash Murmur3.
* [Closure Table](https://github.com/florinpatrascu/closure_table) ⭐ 37 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-07-04 - Closure Table for Elixir - a simple solution for storing and manipulating complex hierarchies. It provides in-memory and Ecto adapters.
* [red\_black\_tree](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/red_black_tree) ⭐ 37 | 🐛 7 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-07-11 - Red-Black tree implementation in Elixir.
* [array](https://github.com/takscape/elixir-array) ⭐ 36 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-10-31 - An Elixir wrapper library for Erlang's array.
* [bitmap](https://github.com/hashd/bitmap-elixir) ⭐ 36 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-01-03 - Pure Elixir implementation of [bitmaps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bitmap).
* [exor\_filter](https://github.com/mpope9/exor_filter) ⭐ 36 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 C | 📅 2021-12-02 - Nif for xor\_filters.  'Faster and Smaller Than Bloom and Cuckoo Filters'.
* [bimap](https://github.com/mkaput/elixir-bimap) ⭐ 34 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-10-21 - Pure Elixir implementation of [bidirectional maps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bidirectional_map) and multimaps.
* [combination](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-combination) ⭐ 34 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-02-25 - Elixir library to generate combinations and permutations from Enumerable collection.
* [eastar](https://github.com/herenowcoder/eastar) ⭐ 34 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-03-10 - A\* graph pathfinding in pure Elixir.
* [qex](https://github.com/princemaple/elixir-queue) ⭐ 34 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-02-14 - Wraps `:queue`, with improved API and `Inspect`, `Collectable` and `Enumerable` protocol implementations.
* [def\_memo](https://github.com/os6sense/DefMemo) ⭐ 32 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-03-12 - A memoization macro (defmemo) for elixir using a genserver backing store.
* [paratize](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-paratize) ⭐ 29 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-02-25 - Elixir library providing some handy parallel processing (execution) facilities that support configuring number of workers and timeout.
* [tinymt](https://github.com/jj1bdx/tinymt-erlang/) ⚠️ Archived - Tiny Mersenne Twister (TinyMT) for Erlang.
* [hash\_ring\_ex](https://github.com/reset/hash-ring-ex) ⭐ 24 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-02-24 - A consistent hash-ring implementation for Elixir.
* [simhash](https://github.com/UniversalAvenue/simhash-ex) ⚠️ Archived - Simhash implementation using Siphash and N-grams.
* [sorted\_set](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/sorted_set) ⭐ 23 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-05-22 - Sorted Sets for Elixir.
* [clope](https://github.com/ayrat555/clope) ⭐ 22 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-07-14 - Elixir implementation of CLOPE: A Fast and Effective Clustering Algorithm for Transactional Data.
* [hypex](https://github.com/whitfin/hypex) ⭐ 21 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-01-02 - Fast Elixir implementation of HyperLogLog.
* [indifferent](https://github.com/vic/indifferent) ⭐ 20 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-07-15 - Indifferent access for Elixir maps/list/tuples with custom key conversion.
* [elistrix](https://github.com/tobz/elistrix) ⭐ 19 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-05-08 - A latency / fault tolerance library to help isolate your applications from an uncertain world of slow or failed services.
* [zipper\_tree](https://github.com/Dkendal/zipper_tree) ⭐ 19 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-03-08 - Variadic arity tree with a zipper for Elixir.
* [nary\_tree](https://github.com/medhiwidjaja/nary_tree) ⭐ 18 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-11-19 - An Elixir implementation of generic n-ary tree data structure.
* [supermemo](https://github.com/edubkendo/supermemo) ⭐ 18 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-02-05 - An Elixir implementation of the [Supermemo 2 algorithm](https://www.supermemo.com/english/ol/sm2.htm).
* [tfidf](https://github.com/OCannings/tf-idf) ⭐ 18 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-03-03 - An Elixir implementation of term frequency–inverse document frequency.
* [luhn](https://github.com/ma2gedev/luhn_ex) ⭐ 17 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2023-01-04 - Luhn algorithm in Elixir.
* [natural\_sort](https://github.com/DanCouper/natural_sort) ⭐ 14 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2021-04-14 - Elixir natural sort implementation for lists of strings.
* [structurez](https://github.com/hamiltop/structurez) ⭐ 14 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-09-09 - A playground for data structures in Elixir.
* [exfsm](https://github.com/awetzel/exfsm) ⭐ 12 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-09-16 - Simple elixir library to define a static FSM.
* [graphex](https://github.com/stocks29/graphex) ⭐ 12 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-09-14 - A library for composing and executing task graphs in elixir.
* [jumper](https://github.com/whitfin/jumper) ⭐ 12 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2023-08-30 - Jump consistent hash implementation in Elixir (without NIFs).
* [mason](https://github.com/spacepilots/mason) ⭐ 12 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-06-21 - Coerce maps into structs. This is helpful e.g. when you interface a REST API and want to create a struct from the response.
* [rock](https://github.com/ayrat555/rock) ⭐ 12 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-07-14 - Elixir implementation of ROCK: A Robust Clustering Algorithm for Categorical Attributes.
* [qrational](https://github.com/q60/rational) ⭐ 9 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-04-29 - Elixir library implementing rational numbers and math operations for them.
* [rendezvous](https://github.com/timdeputter/Rendezvous) ⭐ 9 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-11-19 - Implementation of the Rendezvous or Highest Random Weight (HRW) hashing algorithm in Elixir.
* [lfsr](https://github.com/pma/lfsr) ⭐ 8 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-11-28 - Elixir implementation of a binary Galois Linear Feedback Shift Register.
* [key2value](https://github.com/okeuday/key2value) ⭐ 7 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2023-10-26 - Erlang 2-way Set Associative Map.
* [qcomplex](https://github.com/q60/complex) ⭐ 6 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-04-29 - Elixir library implementing complex numbers and math operations for them.
* [dlist](https://github.com/stocks29/dlist) ⭐ 5 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-03-09 - Deque implementations in Elixir.
* [fnv](https://github.com/asaaki/fnv.ex) ⭐ 5 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-07-04 - Pure Elixir implementation of Fowler–Noll–Vo hash functions.
* [isaac](https://github.com/arianvp/elixir-isaac) ⭐ 4 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-03-29 - Isaac is an elixir module for ISAAC: a fast cryptographic random number generator.
* [minmaxlist](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-minmaxlist) ⭐ 4 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-02-25 - Elixir library extending `Enum.min_by/2`, `Enum.max_by/2` and `Enum.min_max_by/2` to return a list of results instead of just one.
* [mmath](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/mmath) ⭐ 4 | 🐛 5 | 🌐 Erlang | 📅 2018-08-14 - A library for performing math on number 'arrays' in binaries.
* [count\_buffer](https://github.com/camshaft/count_buffer) ⭐ 2 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-12-08 - Buffer a large set of counters and flush periodically.
* [navigation\_tree](https://github.com/gutschilla/elixir-navigation-tree) ⭐ 2 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-09-08 - A navigation tree representation with helpers to generate HTML out of it.
* [spacesaving](https://github.com/rozap/spacesaving) ⭐ 2 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-04-11 - stream count distinct element estimation using the "space saving" algorithm.
* [ezcryptex](https://github.com/stocks29/ezcryptex) ⭐ 0 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2015-07-27 - Thin layer on top of Cryptex.
* [data\_morph](https://hex.pm/packages/data_morph) - Create Elixir structs from data.

## Applications

*Standalone applications.*

* [Phoenix Trello](https://github.com/bigardone/phoenix-trello) ⭐ 2,495 | 🐛 21 | 🌐 JavaScript | 📅 2018-11-09 - Trello tribute done in Elixir, Phoenix Framework, React and Redux.
* [Plural](https://github.com/pluralsh/plural) ⭐ 1,483 | 🐛 53 | 🌐 HTML | 📅 2026-03-06 - Deploys your favorite open source applications like airflow and airbyte in your own cloud account with just two commands.  Written in Elixir and Phoenix Framework for server side, and React for frontend.
* [poxa](https://github.com/edgurgel/poxa) ⭐ 1,084 | 🐛 13 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-06-30 - Open Pusher implementation, compatible with Pusher libraries.
* [RemoteRetro](https://github.com/stride-nyc/remote_retro) ⭐ 585 | 🐛 52 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-07 - A real-time application for conducting Agile retrospectives at [remoteretro.org](https://remoteretro.org) written in Elixir/Phoenix/React.
* [Phoenix Battleship](https://github.com/bigardone/phoenix-battleship) ⭐ 525 | 🐛 7 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-10-01 - The Good Old game built with Elixir, Phoenix Framework, React and Redux.
* [Tai](https://github.com/fremantle-capital/tai) ⭐ 493 | 🐛 11 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-12-07 - A composable, real time, cryptocurrency market data and trade execution toolkit.
* [Lynx](https://github.com/clivern/lynx) ⭐ 367 | 🐛 21 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-09 - A Fast, Secure and Reliable Terraform Backend, Set up in Minutes.
* [exchat](https://github.com/tony612/exchat) ⭐ 259 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-08-28 - A Slack-like app by Elixir, Phoenix & React (redux).
* [ExShop](https://github.com/authentic-pixels/ex-shop) ⭐ 223 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-10-04 - Digital goods shop & blog created using Phoenix framework.
* [CaptainFact](https://github.com/CaptainFact/captain-fact-api) ⭐ 189 | 🐛 29 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-07 - A collaborative, real-time video fact-checking platform. ([Docs](https://captainfact.io/)).
* [Sprint Poker](https://github.com/elpassion/sprint-poker) ⭐ 179 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-08-22 - Online estimation tool for Agile teams, written using Elixir Lang, Phoenix Framework and React.
* [Phoenix Toggl](https://github.com/bigardone/phoenix-toggl) ⭐ 172 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-09-24 - Toggl tribute done in Elixir, Phoenix Framework, React and Redux.
* [tty2048](https://github.com/lexmag/tty2048) ⭐ 156 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-06-16 - Terminal-based 2048 game written in Elixir.
* [Consolex](https://github.com/sivsushruth/consolex) ⭐ 125 | 🐛 3 | 🌐 JavaScript | 📅 2016-06-10 - Consolex is a tool that allows you to attach a web based console to any mix project.

## Geolocation

## Languages

* [exkanji](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/exkanji) ⭐ 14 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-05-13 - A Elixir library for translating between hiragana, katakana, romaji and kanji. It uses Mecab.
* [exromaji](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/exromaji) ⭐ 9 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2018-05-13 - A Elixir library for translating between hiragana, katakana and romaji.
* [getatrex](https://github.com/alexfilatov/getatrex) ⭐ 8 | 🐛 2 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-01-27 - Automatic translation tool of Gettext locales with Google Translate for Elixir/Phoenix projects.
* [parabaikElixirConverter](https://github.com/Arkar-Aung/ParabaikElixirConverter) ⭐ 3 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-03-03 - ParabaikElixirConverter is just a Elixir version of Parabaik converter. It can convert from Unicode to Zawgyi-One and Zawgyi-One to Unicode vice versa.
* [free PO editor](https://pofile.net/free-po-editor) - A tool for translating PO files.

# Resources

Various resources, such as books, websites and articles, for improving your Elixir development skills and knowledge.

## Books

*Fantastic books and e-books.*

* [Études for Elixir](https://www.oreilly.com/library/view/etudes-for-elixir/9781491917640/) - A collection of exercises to program in Elixir by J. David Eisenberg (2013) ([Github Repo](https://github.com/oreillymedia/etudes-for-elixir) ⭐ 519 | 🐛 18 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2022-02-17).
* [Async Elixir](https://github.com/Arp-G/async-elixir) ⭐ 178 | 🐛 2 | 📅 2024-08-08 - Dive into Elixir's world of concurrency and processes with this interactive Livebook.
* [Getting Started - Elixir](https://github.com/potatogopher/elixir-getting-started) ⭐ 101 | 🐛 1 | 📅 2016-08-03 - PDF, MOBI, and EPUB documents for Elixir's Getting Started tutorial (2016).
* [Adopting Elixir](https://pragprog.com/book/tvmelixir/adopting-elixir) - Bring Elixir into your company, with real-life strategies from the people who built Elixir and use it successfully at scale. This book has all the information you need to take your application from concept to production (2017).
* [Craft GraphQL APIs in Elixir with Absinthe](https://pragprog.com/book/wwgraphql/craft-graphql-apis-in-elixir-with-absinthe) - Upgrade your web API to GraphQL, leveraging its flexible queries to empower your users, and its declarative structure to simplify your code (2017).
* [Elixir Cookbook](https://www.packtpub.com/application-development/elixir-cookbook) - This book is a set of recipes grouped by topic by Paulo A Pereira (2015).
* [Elixir do zero à concorrência](https://www.casadocodigo.com.br/products/livro-elixir) - (Portuguese) The book provides introduction to functional and concurrent programming with Elixir by Tiago Davi (2014).
* [Elixir in Action](https://www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action) - A brief intro to the language followed by a more detailed look at building production-ready systems in Elixir by Saša Jurić (2015).
* [Elixir in Action, Second Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action-second-edition) - Revised and updated for Elixir 1.7, Elixir in Action, Second Edition teaches you how to apply Elixir to practical problems associated with scalability, fault tolerance, and high availability (2019).
* [Elixir in Action, Third Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action-third-edition) - Fully updated to Elixir 1.14, this authoritative bestseller reveals how Elixir tackles problems of scalability, fault tolerance, and high availability (2023).
* [Elixir Succinctly](https://www.syncfusion.com/ebooks/elixir-succinctly) - A short book to learn the basic of Elixir and its ecosystem.
* [Engineering Elixir Applications](https://pragprog.com/titles/beamops/engineering-elixir-applications/) - *(currently in Beta)* As the subtitle suggests, this book explores the technologies and skills that support navigating each stage of software delivery with confidence.
* [Erlang and Elixir for Imperative Programmers](https://leanpub.com/erlangandelixirforimperativeprogrammers) - Introduction to Erlang and Elixir in the context of functional concepts by Wolfgang Loder (2016).
* [Erlang in Anger](http://www.erlang-in-anger.com/) - This book intends to be a little guide about how to be the Erlang medic in a time of war by Fred Hebert (2014).
* [Functional Web Development with Elixir, OTP, and Phoenix](https://pragprog.com/book/lhelph/functional-web-development-with-elixir-otp-and-phoenix) - Open doors to powerful new techniques that will get you thinking about web development in fundamentally new ways (2017).
* [Hands-on Elixir & OTP: Cryptocurrency trading bot](https://www.elixircryptobot.com) - Want to learn Elixir & OTP by creating a real-world project? With Hands-on *Elixir & OTP: Cryptocurrency trading bot* you will gain hands-on experience by working on an interesting software project. We will explore all the key abstractions and essential principles through iterative implementation improvements. (2021).
* [Introducing Elixir ](http://shop.oreilly.com/product/0636920030584.do) - A gentle introduction to the language, with lots of code examples and exercises by Simon St. Laurent and J. David Eisenberg (2013).
* [Learn Functional Programming with Elixir](https://pragprog.com/book/cdc-elixir/learn-functional-programming-with-elixir) - Don’t board the Elixir train with an imperative mindset! To get the most out of functional languages, you need to think functionally (2017).
* [Metaprogramming Elixir: Write Less Code, Get More Done (and Have Fun!)](https://pragprog.com/book/cmelixir/metaprogramming-elixir) - Thorough explanation on how to exploit Elixir's metaprogramming capabilities to improve your Elixir coding by Chris McCord (2015).
* [Phoenix for Rails Developers](http://www.phoenixforrailsdevelopers.com) - This book shows how Rails developers can benefit from their existing knowledge to learn Phoenix. By Elvio Vicosa (2017).
* [Phoenix in Action](https://manning.com/books/phoenix-in-action) - builds on your existing web dev skills, teaching you the unique benefits of Phoenix along with just enough Elixir to get the job done. By Geoffrey Lessel (2017).
* [Phoenix Inside Out](https://shankardevy.com/phoenix-book/) - The goal of this series is to enable you as a Confident Phoenix developer. There are 3 different editions to address varied needs of devs jumping into Phoenix.
* [Programming Elixir 1.6](https://pragprog.com/titles/elixir16/) - The book provides introduction to functional and concurrent programming with Elixir by Dave Thomas (2014).
* [Programming Phoenix 1.4](https://pragprog.com/titles/phoenix14/) - Definitive guide to build web applications with the Phoenix framework by Chris McCord, José Valim and Bruce Tate (2015).
* [The Beam Book](https://happi.github.io/theBeamBook/) - A description of the Erlang Runtime System ERTS and the virtual Machine BEAM.
* [The Little Elixir & OTP Guidebook](https://www.manning.com/books/the-little-elixir-and-otp-guidebook) - A book for learning Elixir and OTP through small to medium-sized projects by Benjamin Tan Wei Hao (2014).
* [The Phoenix LiveView Cookbook](https://www.liveviewcookbook.com/) - A Phoenix LiveView e-book containing tried and tested recipes for solving common problems.

## Cheat Sheets

*Useful Elixir-related cheat sheets.*

* [benjamintanweihao/elixir-cheatsheets](https://github.com/benjamintanweihao/elixir-cheatsheets/) ⭐ 107 | 🐛 2 | 📅 2016-09-28 - GenServer and Supervisor cheatsheets.
* [elixir-lang/elixir](https://hexdocs.pm/elixir/main/enum-cheat.html) - Enum cheatsheets.

## Community

*Getting in contact with the community via chat or mailinglist.*

* [Elixir Forum](https://elixirforum.com/) - Community run discussion forums for all things Elixir.
* [elixir-lang-core](https://groups.google.com/d/forum/elixir-lang-core) - Mailinglist for Elixir Core development, use "talk" for questions and general discussions.
* [elixir-lang-talk](https://groups.google.com/d/forum/elixir-lang-talk) - Official Elixir Mailinglist for questions and discussions.
* [ElixirSlack](https://elixir-slackin.herokuapp.com/) - Elixir Slack Community.

* [vim-ex\_test](https://github.com/moofish32/vim-ex_test) ⭐ 4 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 VimL | 📅 2015-10-06 - Vim test runner based on Thoughtbots vim-rspec.
* [vscode-elixir](https://github.com/mat-mcloughlin/vscode-elixir) ⭐ 4 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2017-08-28 - Elixir Support for Visual Studio Code.
* [Atom](https://atom.io/packages/language-elixir) - Elixir language support for Atom.

## Newsletters

*Useful Elixir-related newsletters.*

* [Elixir Digest](http://elixirdigest.net) - A weekly newsletter with the latest articles on Elixir and Phoenix.
* [Elixir Merge](https://elixirmerge.com) - A daily newsletter which delivers two curated updates (articles, tutorials, videos, podcasts) in each edition in quick-read format.
* [Elixir Radar](http://plataformatec.com.br/elixir-radar) - The "official" Elixir newsletter, published weekly via email by Plataformatec.
* [ElixirWeekly](https://elixirweekly.net) - The Elixir community newsletter, covering stuff you easily miss, shared on [ElixirStatus](http://elixirstatus.com) and the web.

## Reading

*Elixir-related reading materials.*

* [Elixir Code Smells](https://github.com/lucasvegi/Elixir-Code-Smells) ⭐ 1,507 | 🐛 1 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2024-09-12 - A catalog of Elixir-specific code smells that can harm the quality of software developed using this language.
* [xElixir](https://github.com/exercism/xelixir) ⭐ 656 | 🐛 7 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-11 - Exercism Exercises in Elixir.
* [Elixir Functional Programming](https://github.com/kblake/functional-programming) ⭐ 361 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2020-06-13 - Material to introduce functional programming using the Elixir language.
* [The Little Schemer in Elixir](https://github.com/jwhiteman/a-little-elixir-goes-a-long-way) ⭐ 345 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2016-01-14 - Exercises and algorithms from the Little Schemer book, ported to Elixir.
* [Elixir Refactorings](https://github.com/lucasvegi/Elixir-Refactorings) ⭐ 189 | 🐛 4 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2025-05-08 - A catalog of refactoring strategies to promote the redesign and improve the quality of code developed with Elixir.
* [Elixir Tab](https://github.com/efexen/elixir-tab) ⭐ 106 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 JavaScript | 📅 2020-01-06 - Chrome Extension which helps you learn the Elixir core lib.
* [Discover Elixir & Phoenix](https://www.ludu.co/course/discover-elixir-phoenix/) - An online course that teaches both the Elixir language and the Phoenix framework.
* [Elixir Cheat-Sheet](http://media.pragprog.com/titles/elixir/ElixirCheat.pdf) - A Elixir cheat sheet, by Andy Hunt & Dave Thomas.
* [Elixir School](https://elixirschool.com/) - Lessons about the Elixir programming language.
* [Elixir vs Ruby | How Switching To Elixir Made Our Team Better](https://foxbox.com/blog/elixir-vs-ruby/) - Long-form post that explains in detail when and why you should choose Elixir over Ruby.
* [Learn With Me: Elixir](https://inquisitivedeveloper.com/tag/lwm-elixir/) - A series where I learn Elixir and you can learn along with me.

## Screencasts

*Cool video tutorials.*

* [Alchemist Camp](https://alchemist.camp) - Alchemist.Camp has many hours of free, project-based Elixir-learning screencasts.
* [Confreaks (Elixir)](http://confreaks.tv/tags/40) - Elixir related conference talks.
* [Curso de Elixir de 0 a 100](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-K74G9nlzSY\&list=PLMLox3fRb_I4_4-DnU3yS_EglDAuVpeEg) - Complete course of elixir (in spanish) for free.
* [Elixir for Programmers](https://codestool.coding-gnome.com/courses/elixir-for-programmers) - Functional, Parallel, Reliable (and fun!), taught by Dave Thomas.
* [Elixir Foundation](https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLjQo0sojbbxXc4aWg5i2umjv7U8YDoHQT) - Learn Elixir by building a practical example. Learn how GenServer, Agents and many other elixir primitives work.
* [Elixir Sips](http://elixirsips.com/) - Tiny screencasts for learning Elixir.
* [ElixirCasts.io](https://elixircasts.io/) - Simple screencasts to help you learn Elixir and Phoenix.
* [ExCasts](https://excasts.com) - Elixir and Phoenix screencasts for all skill levels.
* [Kamil Skowron](https://www.youtube.com/c/kamilskowron) - YouTube channel dedicated to promote functional programming, publishing "real world" programming videos in Elixir like "Hands-on Elixir & OTP: Cryptocurrency trading bot" series.
* [LearnElixir.tv](https://www.learnelixir.tv/) - Beginner friendly, in-depth, step by step screencasts.
* [LearnPhoenix.tv](https://www.learnphoenix.tv/) - Learn how to build fast, dependable web apps with Phoenix.
* [Meet Elixir](https://www.pluralsight.com/courses/meet-elixir) - Walk through some features and concepts of Elixir by José Valim.

## Websites

*Useful Elixir-related websites.*

* [Elixir Github Repository](https://github.com/elixir-lang/elixir) ⭐ 26,532 | 🐛 32 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-11 - The project repository.
* [Elixir Github Wiki](https://github.com/elixir-lang/elixir/wiki) ⭐ 26,532 | 🐛 32 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2026-03-11 - The project's wiki, containing much useful information.
* [30 Days of Elixir](https://github.com/seven1m/30-days-of-elixir) ⭐ 3,064 | 🐛 0 | 🌐 Elixir | 📅 2022-04-13 - A walk through the Elixir language in 30 exercises.
* [BEAM Community](http://beamcommunity.github.io/) - From distributed systems, to robust servers and language design on the Erlang VM.
* [Benjamin Tan - Learnings & Writings](http://benjamintan.io/blog/tags/elixir/) - A blog consisting of mostly Elixir posts.
* [Elixir Career](https://elixir.career/) - A job board for Elixir, and community of Elixir developers.
* [Elixir Examples](http://elixir-examples.github.io/) - A collection of small Elixir programming language examples.
* [Elixir Flashcards](https://elixircards.co.uk/) - Flashcards are a powerful way to improve your knowledge. Elixircards are hand crafted, professionally printed flashcards for levelling up your Elixir.
* [Elixir Online Courses list - Classpert](https://classpert.com/elixir-programming) - A list of Elixir Online Courses (some are free) from Classpert Online Course Search.
* [Elixir Quiz](http://elixirquiz.github.io/) - Weekly programming problems to help you learn Elixir.
* [Elixir Recipes](http://elixir-recipes.github.io/) - Collection of patterns & solutions to common problems in Elixir.
* [ElixirLibs](https://elixirlibs.com) - A curated list of Elixir libraries.
* [Hashrocket Today I Learned - Elixir](https://til.hashrocket.com/elixir) - Small posts about Elixir from the team at Hashrocket.
* [How I start - Elixir](http://howistart.org/posts/elixir/1) - Explanation and intro to Elixir by José Valim.
* [Learning Elixir](http://learningelixir.joekain.com/) - A blog about a Professional Software Engineer learning Elixir.
